[2023/04/08 07:16:47] SQL Query: SELECT 
        c1.name_category AS category1, c1.url AS url1,
        IFNULL(c2.name_category, '') AS category2,
        IFNULL(c2.url, '') AS url2
    FROM 
        products p
        JOIN categories c1 ON p.category_id = c1.id_category
        LEFT JOIN (
            SELECT 
                c1.id_category AS id_category, 
                c2.name_category AS name_category, 
                c2.url AS url 
            FROM categories c1
